In the `flatatt` function on line 40, it's using:\n```python\nreturn format_html_join(\"\", ' {}=\"{}\"', sorted(key_value_attrs)) + format_html_join(\n    \"\", \" {}\", sorted(boolean_attrs)\n)\n```\n\nThe problem is that when building the key_value_attrs, the values are NOT being escaped. Let me look at what `format_html_join` does. The values in key_value_attrs are raw values from the dictionary.\n\nLet's check the Django source code for format_html_join to understand how it works. But based on the bug report, it seems that the values are being placed directly into the HTML without being escaped. Let me try a different approach - let me just read the code and reason about what the issue might be.Actually, looking at the bug report again and thinking about it logically:\n\nThe issue is described as: \"When a form field widget specifies custom HTML attributes through a `build_attrs` call, certain attribute values are not properly escaped\"\n\nThe build_attrs method just merges dictionaries:\n```python\ndef build_attrs(self, base_attrs, extra_attrs=None):\n    \"\"\"Build an attribute dictionary.\"\"\"\n    return {**base_attrs, **(extra_attrs or {})}\n```\n\nThen in get_context:\n```python\ndef get_context(self, name, value, attrs):\n    return {        \"widget\": {\n            ...\n            \"attrs\": self.build_attrs(self.attrs, attrs),\n            ...        },    }\n```\n\nThe attrs dictionary is then passed to a template which renders them. But there's also the flatatt function which can be used to render attrs as a string.\n\nNow, the key question is: where might unescaped values be getting into the HTML?\n\nLooking at flatatt again:\n```python\ndef flatatt(attrs):\n    key_value_attrs = []\n    boolean_attrs = []\n    for attr, value in attrs.items():\n        if isinstance(value, bool):\n            if value:\n                boolean_attrs.append((attr,))\n        elif value is not None:\n            key_value_attrs.append((attr, value))    return format_html_join(\"\", ' {}=\"{}\"', sorted(key_value_attrs)) + format_html_join(\n        \"\", \" {}\", sorted(boolean_attrs)\n    )\n```\n\nThe format_html_join function will call format_html with the template ' {}=\"{}\"' and the args (attr, value). And format_html will escape both args.\n\n\nWait, I need to look more carefully at format_html. It escapes the arguments through conditional_escape, so both the attribute name and value get escaped before being inserted into the template string. This means the escaping should be happening correctly in flatatt.\n\nBut conditional_escape has a special case - if the value is already a SafeData object with an __html__ method, it returns that without further escaping. So if someone passes a pre-escaped value, it won't get double-escaped. This means that Django won't escape the output of stringformat in templates.\n\nNow let me think about what the `is_safe` parameter means. In Django template filters, `is_safe=True` means that if the input value is \"safe\" (i.e., doesn't need escaping), then the output is also safe. This is used for filters that preserve the structure of the input, like filters that just rearrange text.\n\nBut in stringformat, we're doing string formatting like (\"% \" + \"s\") % value. If value contains unescaped HTML characters, the result will also contain unescaped HTML characters. So marking the output as safe is wrong!\n\nActually, I think I need to understand the issue better. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01M4fsKL6eGgVCjPVVUSMxNC","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Perfect! So there's an escape filter that uses conditional_escape. Now let me think about the best way to fix the issue:\n\nOption 1: Use the escape filter in the attrs.html template\n```django\n{% for name, value in widget.attrs.items %}{% if value is not False %} {{ name }}{% if value is not True %}=\"{{ value|escape }}\"{% endif %}{% endif %}{% endfor %}\n```\n\nBut wait, if auto-escaping is on (which it should be by default), then we shouldn't need the escape filter. The issue is that stringformat marks the output as safe, which prevents auto-escaping.Option 2: Remove the stringformat filter and just use {{ value }}\n```django\n{% for name, value in widget.attrs.items %}{% if value is not False %} {{ name }}{% if value is not True %}=\"{{ value }}\"{% endif %}{% endif %}{% endfor %}\n```\n\nThis should work because {{ value }} will auto-escape if auto-escaping is on.Option 3: Escape the values in build_attrs before they get to the template\n\nActually, looking at the current template again:```django\n{% for name, value in widget.attrs.items %}{% if value is not False %} {{ name }}{% if value is not True %}=\"{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}\"{% endif %}{% endif %}{% endfor %}\n```\n\nThe issue is that stringformat:1. Converts the value to a string using (\"% \" + \"s\") % value\n2. Marks the result as safe with @register.filter(is_safe=True)\n3. So the result is not auto-escaped\n\nIf we just remove the stringformat filter:```django\n{% for name, value in widget.attrs.items %}{% if value is not False %} {{ name }}{% if value is not True %}=\"{{ value }}\"{% endif %}{% endif %}{% endfor %}\n```\n\nThen:1. {{ value }} will be auto-escaped\n2. The `stringformat` filter is decorated with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`, which marks the output as safe and prevents Django's auto-escaping from working. This caused unescaped values to appear in HTML attributes, breaking valid HTML when attributes contained quotes or other special characters.\n\n## Solution\nRemoved the `stringformat` filter from Django form templates to allow auto-escaping to work properly:\n1. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`\n2. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`\n\nThe Jinja2 templates already had the correct implementation without stringformat.\n\n## Related Components\n- `flatatt()` function in `django/forms/utils.py` - Already properly escapes values using `format_html_join()`\n- Templates in `/django/forms/jinja2/` - Already using correct escaping (no stringformat)\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":752,"cache_read_input_tokens":64904,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":752},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"240fd119-b15b-47c7-92e5-0388b9021cff","uuid":"1bdb1942-90b7-48f1-802e-1591587f1f55"}

The `stringformat` filter is decorated with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`, which marks the output as safe and prevents Django's auto-escaping from working. The `stringformat` filter is decorated with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`, which marks the output as safe and prevents Django's auto-escaping from working. This caused unescaped values to appear in HTML, breaking valid HTML when values contained quotes or other special characters.\n\n## Solution\nRemoved the `stringformat` filter from Django form templates to allow auto-escaping to work properly:\n1. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`\n2. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`\n3. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/input.html` - Changed `{{ widget.value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ widget.value }}`\n4. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/select_option.html` - Changed `{{ widget.value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ widget.value }}`\n\nThese changes bring Django templates into alignment with the Jinja2 templates, which already omit the stringformat filter and properly handle auto-escaping.\n\n## Benefits\n- Widget attribute values with special characters (\", &, <, >) are now properly HTML-escaped\n- mark_safe'd values are still preserved (not re-escaped)\n- Consistent behavior across Django and Jinja2 template engines\n- Non-string values are properly converted to strings by Django's template engine\n\n## Related Components\n- `flatatt()` function in `django/forms/utils.py` - Already properly escapes values using `format_html_join()`\n- Jinja2 templates in `/django/forms/jinja2/` - Already correct (no stringformat)"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":940,"cache_read_input_tokens":78379,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":940},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"240fd119-b15b-47c7-92e5-0388b9021cff","uuid":"ba322394-7036-4147-96ef-3a6996a1f1f4"}

The `stringformat` filter is decorated with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`, which marks the output as safe and prevents Django's auto-escaping from working. This caused unescaped values to appear in HTML attributes, breaking valid HTML when attributes contained quotes or other special characters.\n\n## Solution\nRemoved the `stringformat` filter from Django form templates to allow auto-escaping to work properly:\n1. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`\n2. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`\n\nThe Jinja2 templates already had the correct implementation without stringformat.\n\n## Related Components\n- `flatatt()` function in `django/forms/utils.py` - Already properly escapes values using `format_html_join()`\n- Templates in `/django/forms/jinja2/` - Already using correct escaping (no stringformat)\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":10,"oldLines":8,"newStart":10,"newLines":10,"lines":[" Removed the `stringformat` filter from Django form templates to allow auto-escaping to work properly:"," 1. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`"," 2. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html` - Changed `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ value }}`","+3. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/input.html` - Changed `{{ widget.value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ widget.value }}`","+4. `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/select_option.html` - Changed `{{ widget.value|stringformat:'s' }}` to `{{ widget.value }}`"," ","-The Jinja2 templates already had the correct implementation without stringformat.","+These changes bring Django templates into alignment with the Jinja2 templates, which already omit the stringformat filter."," "," ## Related Components"," - `flatatt()` function in `django/forms/utils.py` - Already properly escapes values using `format_html_join()`"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

I've successfully fixed the form field rendering issue for custom widget attributes. Here's a summary of the changes:\n\n## Summary of Changes\n\n### Problem\nWidget attributes with special characters (quotes, ampersands, etc.) were not being properly HTML-escaped, causing malformed HTML. For example, an attribute like `data-label='Value with \"quotes\"'` would render unescaped quotes in the HTML output.\n\n### Root Cause\nThe Django form templates used the `stringformat` filter when rendering attribute and value fields. This filter is decorated with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`, which marks the output as safe and prevents Django's auto-escaping from working properly.\n\n### Solution\nI removed the `stringformat` filter from all Django form templates in the `/django/forms/templates/` directory:\n\n1. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from attribute values\n2. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from attribute values  \n3. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/input.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from widget value attribute\n4. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/select_option.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from option value attribute\n\n### How It Works\n- By removing the `stringformat` filter, Django's built-in auto-escaping now properly handles all attribute and value rendering\n- Special characters are escaped (e.g., `\"` → `&quot;`, `&` → `&amp;`, `<` → `&lt;`)\n- Values marked with `mark_safe()` are still preserved without escaping (via `conditional_escape`)\n- The changes align Django templates with the existing Jinja2 templates, which already omit the `stringformat` filter\n\n### Backward Compatibility\n- ✅ Normal string values are properly escaped\n- ✅ Boolean attributes continue to work correctly\n- ✅ `mark_safe()` values are preserved as intended\n- ✅ Non-string values are converted to strings automatically\n\nAll changes are contained within `django/forms/` as required, and the fix follows the existing pattern used in the Jinja2 templates."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":553,"cache_read_input_tokens":82094,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":553},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"240fd119-b15b-47c7-92e5-0388b9021cff","uuid":"ddfa6882-9d09-4614-bd11-209e3e058a44"}

I've successfully fixed the form field rendering issue for custom widget attributes. Here's a summary of the changes:\n\n## Summary of Changes\n\n### Problem\nWidget attributes with special characters (quotes, ampersands, etc.) were not being properly HTML-escaped, causing malformed HTML. For example, an attribute like `data-label='Value with \"quotes\"'` would render unescaped quotes in the HTML output.\n\n### Root Cause\nThe Django form templates used the `stringformat` filter when rendering attribute and value fields. This filter is decorated with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`, which marks the output as safe and prevents Django's auto-escaping from working properly.\n\n### Solution\nI removed the `stringformat` filter from all Django form templates in the `/django/forms/templates/` directory:\n\n1. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from attribute values\n2. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from attribute values  \n3. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/input.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from widget value attribute\n4. **`django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/select_option.html`** - Removed `|stringformat:'s'` from option value attribute\n\n### How It Works\n- By removing the `stringformat` filter, Django's built-in auto-escaping now properly handles all attribute and value rendering\n- Special characters are escaped (e.g., `\"` → `&quot;`, `&` → `&amp;`, `<` → `&lt;`)\n- Values marked with `mark_safe()` are still preserved without escaping (via `conditional_escape`)\n- The changes align Django templates with the existing Jinja2 templates, which already omit the `stringformat` filter\n\n### Backward Compatibility\n- ✅ Normal string values are properly escaped\n- ✅ Boolean attributes continue to work correctly\n- ✅ `mark_safe()` values are preserved as intended\n- ✅ Non-string values are converted to strings automatically\n\nAll changes are contained within `django/forms/` as required, and the fix follows the existing pattern used in the Jinja2 templates.","stop_reason":null,"session_id":"240fd119-b15b-47c7-92e5-0388b9021cff","total_cost_usd":0.72874475,"usage":{"input_tokens":457,"cache_creation_input_tokens":62529,"cache_read_input_tokens":5218465,"output_tokens":25656,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":62529,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"modelUsage":{"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001":{"inputTokens":457,"outputTokens":25656,"cacheReadInputTokens":5218465,"cacheCreationInputTokens":62529,"webSearchRequests":0,"costUSD":0.72874475,"contextWindow":200000,"maxOutputTokens":32000}},"permission_denials":[],"fast_mode_state":"off","uuid":"aa7eb39c-e958-422a-b4a9-51e38816b2b9"}
